<div id="review_2547461578" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2547461578" />
    <a title="Bea" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/68155245-bea"><img alt="Bea" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598741314p2/68155245.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2547461578?book_show_action=true">Dec 07, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bea" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bea" href="/user/show/68155245-bea">Bea</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/12968706-the-well-of-ascension">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68155245-bea?shelf=big-books">big-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68155245-bea?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68155245-bea?shelf=tear-worthy">tear-worthy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68155245-bea?shelf=3-5-star-reads">3-5-star-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68155245-bea?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68155245-bea?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68155245-bea?shelf=sanderson">sanderson</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer2547461578&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2547461578" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6263983044323835766">Even with its annoying faults, I don’t think I can give this less than a <b>3.5 star rating.</b><br/><br/><b>THAT ENDING THOUGH.</b> <br/><br/>Overall I’d say this was a good continuation to the series, this one focuses a lot - like <b>A LOT</b> more on politics than actual action like the first book did. However it also focused on character development for both Vin and Elend, the two main characters which Sanderson managed to do fairly well.<br/><br/>Sazed is my favourite character in this series. Continuing on from the first book he just has a</span>
  <span id="freeText6263983044323835766" style="display:none">Even with its annoying faults, I don’t think I can give this less than a <b>3.5 star rating.</b><br /><br /><b>THAT ENDING THOUGH.</b> <br /><br />Overall I’d say this was a good continuation to the series, this one focuses a lot - like <b>A LOT</b> more on politics than actual action like the first book did. However it also focused on character development for both Vin and Elend, the two main characters which Sanderson managed to do fairly well.<br /><br />Sazed is my favourite character in this series. Continuing on from the first book he just has a heart of gold and most importantly, he loves telling stories and tales! His relationship with Tindwyl, who I loved as a character was also so well developed and beautiful till the very end.<br /><br />My main grudge with this book is that <b>it really didn’t need to be this long.</b> The first 200 pages or so were just.. talking? And the middle of the book was again talking, but with a little more action and then finally, the ending is <b>FULL</b> of action! Less of that beginning would’ve been better! <i>A lot of it really wasn’t needed!</i><br /><br />Another grudge I have is that <b>so much of this was Vin moaning and complaining about her feelings from her relationship with Elend</b> and there was just too much of that in my opinion. She kept and kept on switching between ‘he loves me’.. ‘he loves me not’... and at times it just got irritating. Stop that Vin, <i>he adores you! </i><br /><br />I cried twice during this book, Sazed finding Tindwyl’s body <b>(WHY ARE YOU MESSING WITH MY HEART SANDERSON) </b>and when Elend gets attacked at the Well of Ascension. <i>Soooo many feelings!</i><br /><br /><b>
  <u>Just read this series if you haven’t already.</u>
</b></span>

<div id="review_1843496990" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1843496990" />
    <a title="Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes"><img alt="Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598297811p2/1452829.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1843496990?book_show_action=true">Dec 18, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~" href="/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes">Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes?shelf=year-2016">year-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1843496990" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13770081577867499838"><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/68429.The_Well_of_Ascension__Mistborn___2_' title='The Well of Ascension (Mistborn, #2) by Brandon Sanderson' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Well of Ascension</a> was a beautiful follow-up to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/68428.The_Final_Empire__Mistborn___1_' title='The Final Empire (Mistborn, #1) by Brandon Sanderson' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Final Empire</a>. There's so much going on now that it's difficult to speak on a lot of the specifics, so my review will focus on more <u>general overview</u> of what I enjoyed and what I didn't.<br/><br/><b>
  <u>Plot:</u>
</b><br/><br/>The plot was <i>by far</i> the strongest point of the novel. I was just so engrossed in all of the political conversations happening here. I like my high fantasy heavy on the political intrigue with dashes of cunning & betrayal.<br/><br/>Plus the last little bit of thi</span>
  <span id="freeText13770081577867499838" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/68429.The_Well_of_Ascension__Mistborn___2_" title="The Well of Ascension (Mistborn, #2) by Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">The Well of Ascension</a> was a beautiful follow-up to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/68428.The_Final_Empire__Mistborn___1_" title="The Final Empire (Mistborn, #1) by Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">The Final Empire</a>. There's so much going on now that it's difficult to speak on a lot of the specifics, so my review will focus on more <u>general overview</u> of what I enjoyed and what I didn't.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>Plot:</u>
</b><br /><br />The plot was <i>by far</i> the strongest point of the novel. I was just so engrossed in all of the political conversations happening here. I like my high fantasy heavy on the political intrigue with dashes of cunning &amp; betrayal.<br /><br />Plus the last little bit of this story just <b>blew my fucking mind.</b> Sanderson has no mercy when it comes to plot twists. He'll drag you through the ashes of your favorite characters. He'll throw you out of the airplane and shout <i>"Plot twist! I cut holes in your parachute, bitch!"</i><br /><br />It was crazy! But I enjoyed every minute of this plot as it unfolded. <br /><br /><b>
  <u>Character Development:</u>
</b><br /><br /><b>I feel as though Vin is the only character that really grew at all in this novel.</b> <br /><br />There is an argument to be made for both Sazed and Elend, as they do make some strides forward, but most of the development primarily revolved around Vin. For me, I wanted a <b>little more</b> in this area. I feel like everyone else was static and that didn't really do much for my reading experience.<br /><br />I'm very glad though for all that Vin underwent in this novel because I really wasn't that fond of her in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/68428.The_Final_Empire__Mistborn___1_" title="The Final Empire (Mistborn, #1) by Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">The Final Empire</a>, and so this really helped me sympathize with and understand her as an individual.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>Pace:</u>
</b><br /><br />The pace was just a <i>little</i> bit slow in some places for me. As you may or may not know, I'm not normally very bothered by a slow pace. Like we have to be almost moving backwards before I notice anything is amiss. <br /><br />However, there were just a few parts here that dragged a bit longer than I found necessary. Overall though, I didn't much mind the pace. It's methodical, it's well done, and most of the information presented here is necessary. <br /><br />I'm very excited to start the final book in this trilogy. The last section of this novel has me very anxious to find out how this will all end!<br /><br />Buddy read this with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/5769334-bluelilyxlilyblue" rel="nofollow noopener">sweet Aria</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/35431290-tweebs" rel="nofollow noopener">Tweebsiepoo</a>, &amp; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/29249069-pragya" rel="nofollow noopener">my bby Pragya</a>.<br /><br /><b>*UPDATE: Spoilers in my comments section for The Final Empire!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="13770081577867499838" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer1385491130452481518">The Well of Ascension is the 2nd installment of the famous Mistborn series and, as expected, it suffers from the middle book syndrome. I enjoyed reading the new adventures of Vin and the crew but not as much as in The Final Empire. The majority of the plot revolves around the siege of Luthadel by enemies and the planning to protect the city. While some aspects were interesting I believe the talking went on and on for too long. Secondly, the Vin’s teenage angst and doubts about herself and her re</span>
  <span id="freeText1385491130452481518" style="display:none">The Well of Ascension is the 2nd installment of the famous Mistborn series and, as expected, it suffers from the middle book syndrome. I enjoyed reading the new adventures of Vin and the crew but not as much as in The Final Empire. The majority of the plot revolves around the siege of Luthadel by enemies and the planning to protect the city. While some aspects were interesting I believe the talking went on and on for too long. Secondly, the Vin’s teenage angst and doubts about herself and her relationship with Elend drove me mad after pages and pages of interior debates. <br /><br />I missed Kelsier, I thought that his character was what made the first book shine but I loved Sazed and OreSeur in this one. I also enjoyed the plot twist at the end and I can’t wait to read the final book in the trilogy. <br /></span>

<div id="review_1189197329" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1189197329" />
    <a title="Merna " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16392157-merna"><img alt="Merna " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1358143553p2/16392157.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1189197329?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Merna " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Merna " href="/user/show/16392157-merna">Merna </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780575089938" href="/book/show/6547260-the-well-of-ascension">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16392157-merna?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16392157-merna?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1189197329" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9094998565138976077"><b>This book goes something likes this:</b><br/><br/><b>Elend and the group:</b> Hey, we need to find a way to defeat these two armies, led by tyrants, who've come to conquer the city.<br/><br/><b>Elend and the group:</b>Yes, we should! But first, let us talk about it for 500 pages.<br/><br/>Anyway, I've read many reviews that mention this book is slow paced, but to even describe this book merely 'slow-paced' is a big understatement. I think glacial pace describes it much better. You keep thinking it's going to pick up, after all, it's 700 pages</span>
  <span id="freeText9094998565138976077" style="display:none"><b>This book goes something likes this:</b><br /><br /><b>Elend and the group:</b> Hey, we need to find a way to defeat these two armies, led by tyrants, who've come to conquer the city.<br /><br /><b>Elend and the group:</b>Yes, we should! But first, let us talk about it for 500 pages.<br /><br />Anyway, I've read many reviews that mention this book is slow paced, but to even describe this book merely 'slow-paced' is a big understatement. I think glacial pace describes it much better. You keep thinking it's going to pick up, after all, it's 700 pages, so what if it's slow for the first 200, but no, it had to be slow for nearly 600 pages. <br />Nonetheless, I really liked how well everything ties up at the end. It was planned excellently. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9094998565138976077" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2435805897" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2435805897" />
    <a title="Lyn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5253785-lyn"><img alt="Lyn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1495541962p2/5253785.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2435805897?book_show_action=true">Jun 25, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lyn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lyn" href="/user/show/5253785-lyn">Lyn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2435805897" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10732352937877536996">It’s like this:<br/><br/>You’re excited about the date, it is the second after all. The first date had been fun, lots of good conversation, some intriguing flirtation that might lead to something, but not yet, you’re both getting to know each other. But there were some odd moments too, some talk that led nowhere, some awkward silences, maybe a joke that withered on the vine. The first date had ended well though, with a kiss, not quite chaste but just shy of romantic. So there was some anticipation for thi</span>
  <span id="freeText10732352937877536996" style="display:none">It’s like this:<br><br>You’re excited about the date, it is the second after all. The first date had been fun, lots of good conversation, some intriguing flirtation that might lead to something, but not yet, you’re both getting to know each other. But there were some odd moments too, some talk that led nowhere, some awkward silences, maybe a joke that withered on the vine. The first date had ended well though, with a kiss, not quite chaste but just shy of romantic. So there was some anticipation for this second meeting. More good fun, there is definitely some chemistry … but it’s still not all fitting together, like a puzzle missing some pieces, or like a movie when you missed an important scene getting more popcorn. Still very interested, but the kiss that ended this one was a little more hopeful, or was it?<br><br>Brandon Sanderson’s 2007 second Mistborn is as fun as the first, but I’m still not all in, still “going out” we’re not quite dating yet.<br><br>The Lord Ruler is dead and the power vacuum that follows is well described and entertaining. But it can also be tedious.<br><br>Where Vin was the show stealer in the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/68428.The_Final_Empire__Mistborn___1_" title="The Final Empire (Mistborn, #1) by Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">The Final Empire</a>, Sazed most definitely owns this one. His storyline may actually be one of the best character developments in recent fantasy. His inner angst and doubts were delicious.<br><br>Sanderson continues to build this AWESOME world and expands his COOL AS HELL magic building. I found myself going to Wikipedia to try and learn all the metal rules. Sounds like a School of Rock lesson.<br><br>Is this an anime? I looked online and I’m not the only one who thinks this story would be PERFECT for that medium adaptation.<br><br>Good second date, there will be a third. ;)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1566340182i/28024209.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="10732352937877536996" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('cbwa0Q8UeKAm8ZhwQR1V2NIGoCCXWDk8MvAd67dD/r5lxBcZgBB+Sp7uqmgjLbI0mFK+y5wpL/KCkKWeSl55EA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('SkojTG1CByoGRnIY5+/AiPYG7rezVrtALR6frq1kdbpeMi6E4kYBwL5ZQACF3ydkvFLwXLgnrY6dfifbUHnyFA==')})
  }

While attempting to curry favor with a powerful noble, Kvothe uncovers an assassination attempt, comes into conflict with a rival arcanist, and leads a group of mercenaries into the wild, in an attempt to solve the mystery of who (or what) is waylaying travelers on the King\'s Road.\n\nAll the while, Kvothe searches for answers, attempting to uncover the truth about the mysterious Amyr, the Chandrian, and the death of his parents.       <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/38550.Brandon_Sanderson">About Brandon Sanderson</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/38550.Brandon_Sanderson"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1394044556p3/38550.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/38550.Brandon_Sanderson">Brandon Sanderson
</a></div>
<div class='goodreadsAuthorBadge'></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
154,135
followers
</div>

</div>
</div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer6847441945070668053">Brandon’s major books for the second half of 2016 are <i><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18714787.The_Dark_Talent' title='The Dark Talent' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Dark Talent</a>,</i> the final volume in Alcatraz Smedry’s autobiographical account of his battle against the Evil Librarians who secretly rule our world, and <i><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28595941.Arcanum_Unbounded' title='Arcanum Unbounded' rel='nofollow noopener'>Arcanum Unbounded</a>,</i> the collection of short fiction in the Cosmere universe that includes the Mistborn series and the Stormlight <br/>Archive, among others. This collection features <i><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13578175.The_Emperor_s_Soul' title='The Emperor’s Soul' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Emperor’s S</a></i></span>
  <span id="freeText6847441945070668053" style="display:none">Brandon’s major books for the second half of 2016 are <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18714787.The_Dark_Talent" title="The Dark Talent" rel="nofollow noopener">The Dark Talent</a>,</i> the final volume in Alcatraz Smedry’s autobiographical account of his battle against the Evil Librarians who secretly rule our world, and <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28595941.Arcanum_Unbounded" title="Arcanum Unbounded" rel="nofollow noopener">Arcanum Unbounded</a>,</i> the collection of short fiction in the Cosmere universe that includes the Mistborn series and the Stormlight <br />Archive, among others. This collection features <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13578175.The_Emperor_s_Soul" title="The Emperor’s Soul" rel="nofollow noopener">The Emperor’s Soul</a>,</i> <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28698036.Mistborn__Secret_History" title="Mistborn: Secret History" rel="nofollow noopener">Mistborn: Secret History</a>,</i> and a brand-new Stormlight Archive novella, <i>Edgedancer</i>.<br /><br />Earlier this year he released <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15704486.Calamity" title="Calamity" rel="nofollow noopener">Calamity</a>,</i> the finale of the #1 New York Times bestselling Reckoners trilogy that began with <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17182126.Steelheart" title="Steelheart" rel="nofollow noopener">Steelheart</a>
</i>.<br /><br />Brandon Sanderson was born in 1975 in Lincoln, Nebraska. As a child Brandon enjoyed reading, but he lost interest in the types of titles often suggested to him, and by junior high he never cracked a book if he could help it. This changed when an eighth grade teacher gave him <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/176268.Dragonsbane" title="Dragonsbane" rel="nofollow noopener">Dragonsbane</a>
</i> by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/10333.Barbara_Hambly" title="Barbara Hambly" rel="nofollow noopener">Barbara Hambly</a>.<br /><br />Brandon was working on his thirteenth novel when Moshe Feder at Tor Books bought the sixth he had written. Tor has published <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/68427.Elantris" title="Elantris" rel="nofollow noopener">Elantris</a>,</i> the Mistborn trilogy and its followup <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10803121.The_Alloy_of_Law" title="The Alloy of Law" rel="nofollow noopener">The Alloy of Law</a>,</i> <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1268479.Warbreaker" title="Warbreaker" rel="nofollow noopener">Warbreaker</a>,</i> and <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7235533.The_Way_of_Kings" title="The Way of Kings" rel="nofollow noopener">The Way of Kings</a>
</i> and <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11543195.Words_of_Radiance" title="Words of Radiance" rel="nofollow noopener">Words of Radiance</a>,</i> the first two in the planned ten-volume series The Stormlight Archive. He was chosen to complete <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6252.Robert_Jordan" title="Robert Jordan" rel="nofollow noopener">Robert Jordan</a>’s Wheel of Time series; 2009’s <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1166599.The_Gathering_Storm" title="The Gathering Storm" rel="nofollow noopener">The Gathering Storm</a>
</i> and 2010’s <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8253920.Towers_of_Midnight" title="Towers of Midnight" rel="nofollow noopener">Towers of Midnight</a>
</i> were followed by the final book in the series, <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1166599.A_Memory_of_Light" title="A Memory of Light" rel="nofollow noopener">A Memory of Light</a>,</i> in January 2013. Four books in his middle-grade <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/623976.Alcatraz_vs__the_Evil_Librarians" title="Alcatraz vs. the Evil Librarians" rel="nofollow noopener">Alcatraz vs. the Evil Librarians</a>
</i> series have been released in new editions by Starscape, and his novella <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12796771.Infinity_Blade_Awakening" title="Infinity Blade Awakening" rel="nofollow noopener">Infinity Blade Awakening</a>
</i> was an ebook bestseller for Epic Games accompanying their acclaimed <i>Infinity Blade</i> iOS video game series. Two more novellas, <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13452375.Legion" title="Legion" rel="nofollow noopener">Legion</a>
</i> and <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13578175.The_Emperor_s_Soul" title="The Emperor’s Soul" rel="nofollow noopener">The Emperor’s Soul</a>,</i> were released by Subterranean Press and Tachyon Publications in 2012, and 2013 brought two young adult novels, <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10137823.The_Rithmatist" title="The Rithmatist" rel="nofollow noopener">The Rithmatist</a>
</i> from Tor and <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17182126.Steelheart" title="Steelheart" rel="nofollow noopener">Steelheart</a>
</i> from Delacorte.<br /><br />The only author to make the short list for the David Gemmell Legend Award six times in four years, Brandon won that award in 2011 for <i>The Way of Kings</i>. <i>The Emperor’s Soul</i> won the 2013 Hugo Award for Best Novella. He has appeared on the <i>New York Times</i> Best-Seller List multiple times, with five novels hitting the #1 spot.<br /><br />Currently living in Utah with his wife and children, Brandon teaches creative writing at Brigham Young University.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6847441945070668053" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>

Then, when hope was so long lost that not even its memory remained, a terribly scarred, heart-broken half-Skaa rediscovered it in the depths of the Lord Ruler\'s most hellish prison. Kelsier &quot;snapped&quot; and found in himself the powers of a Mistborn. A brilliant thief and natural leader, he turned his talents to the ultimate caper, with the Lord Ruler himself as the mark.\n\nKelsier recruited the underworld\'s elite, the smartest and most trustworthy allomancers, each of whom shares one of his many powers, and all of whom relish a high-stakes challenge. Only then does he reveal his ultimate dream, not just the greatest heist in history, but the downfall of the divine despot.\n\nBut even with the best criminal crew ever assembled, Kel\'s plan looks more like the ultimate long shot, until luck brings a ragged girl named Vin into his life. Like him, she\'s a half-Skaa orphan, but she\'s lived a much harsher life. Vin has learned to expect betrayal from everyone she meets, and gotten it.
